To show everlasting life through Jesus's sacrifice. John 14:6 states: "Jesus saith unto him, I am the way, the truth, and the life: no man cometh unto the Father, but by me.". Keeping people from thinking about salvation. Keeping you from thinking about life after death. Please, ask Jesus into your hearts to save you of your sins and cleanse you from all unrighteousness. Why no Vin Petrol and Slow & Frustrated?
Thunder rang throughout the streets of Brooklyn, New York, "Give us what we came for, Steven," a man demanded as he stood over a man laid out in a crater. Steven merely smirked from the demand, "Over my dead body," he retorted as anger grew into the man's face, "That could be done," the man stated, lunging towards Steven, closing his eyes to accept his fate.   But the finishing strike never came; opening his eyes once more, Steven saw a man standing over him, stopping the man's attack. "D-d-dad?" Steven questioned as the man looked down at him, "FAILURE," Steven's dad stated as he threw the attacker away.   Recollecting himself, the attacker glared at Steven's dad with dozens of men surrounding the two. "So you are the true protector of Beijing Corn, Steven's dad," the man stated as a bolt of lightning struck only yards away from him. "And you are the one who created Physics, Issac Newton," Steven's dad stated as Issac Newton clenched his fist.   "Steven, you must leave; this battle is not yours to fight; you are too much of a failure to defend the legendary Beijing Corn," Steven's dad stated as he summoned his weapons, summoning the legendary can of Beijing corn and a short-range tree branch, with various slippers floating around him.   Issac Newton picked one hand up, "ATTACK STUDENTS OF PHYSICS," he shouted as a dozen students rushed Steven's dad; the first rushed straight forward, throwing a strike straight for Steven's dad's face.   In the eyes of the father, time slowed, 'one in front with three circlings, I need to dodge first strike and counter by throwing him to the three surroundings,' he thought to himself as he caught the arm and judo threw him into the three circling behind him before sending a slipper to the direction of four more targets knocking them to the floor as he smirked.   "Too easy, eight down and only four more to go," he started as he reeled up his branch before swinging it at two approaching students; they fell to the floor as he merely laughed, "When I went to school, I had to fight two lions a day every day, now they do my taxes. Then I traveled up and downhill 20 miles on one foot at the same time. My other foot was starting a business," he explained beating the last of the students as he stood in front of Issac Newton.   "Then you created Physics," he angrily stated as he glared into the eyes of Newton, who merely placed his hands together. Steven's dad was sent flying as items began to float around Issac Newton, "Steven's dad, you merely have one of the legendary cans; I have the other four," he stated as the four cans were revealed.   First was Shanghai Corn, the can that was once protected by the neighbor, the second was Guangzhou corn protected by an unknown master, the third was the Hongkong Corn, and lastly, Doge corn.   "ALL I NEED IS BEIJING CORN, AND I WILL BE ABLE TO BANISH ALL A's," the man shouted as he aimed his palm towards Steven's dad, pushing the man to the ground before pulling him back.   Holding Steven's dad by the collar, Issac reached for the can but was stopped when Steven's dad placed both hands onto his temple, "EMOTIONAL DAMAGE," he shouted, causing both of their eyes and mouths to glow with white beaming lights.  When Issac opened his eyes, he stood next to Steven's dad in front of a car, "Steven, get me a screwdriver," he demanded; Issac had no control over his body as he found a box filled with different types of screwdrivers. "What is this," he thought to himself as he looked at the box before looking back at Steven's dad.   "Which one?"    "The one in the box,"  "Which one?"  "The one that turns the screw?"  "I know, but which one,"   "THE ONE WITH THE HANDLE," Steven's dad shouted as Issac felt frustrated from the response.  "T-they a-all have handles," he cried out as he fell to the floor in a futile position.   Outside of the mind, Steven's dad stood over the fallen Issac, breathing heavily, "That right there is emotional damage," he stated as he took the last four cans away from Issac.   "D-dad, you won," Steven celebrated before his dad glared at him. "STEVEN YOU'RE A FAILURE,"  THE END
